This farm will work on Bedrock, but don't more then 5 layers as it slows the farm down due to the mobcap on Bedrock. The spawns on this farm would be classed as underground spawns and we can only have 16 underground mobs total at any time. If you know how to make an above ground spawning tear, that doubles the rates as we can have 16 above ground mobs on top of the 16 underground mobs. If you check out @ProwlMinecraft , specifically his general mob farm, he shows how to create an above ground spawning platform.
